Divyam Sharma shared a post: Hi everyone! Really hope that everyone is doing well as the 2nd wave seems to have subsided for a while bringing us all some respite. I just wanted to share the beginning of a new chapter in my life that has started this week. I begin my first job as I have joined the Data Science Team at Micron Technology India at the Hyderabad office on July 12th, sincerely due to the efforts of my recruiter Mohammed Parvez Pasha and the team at Micron and the efforts of the Placement Unit, BITS Pilani, Pilani Campus led by the awesome Placement Managers Tabir Mishra and vipul singhal adding to the magic of my alma mater Birla Institute of Technology and Science, Pilani. The last week went by in the blink of an eye as the NCG's (new college graduates) woke up and attended the beautifully curated Micron Assimilation Program daily beginning sharply at 9 AM and staying on through the day. It truly seems like a long time but the sessions by various leaders such as Anand Ramamoorthy, Koushik Ragavan, Shisheer Kotha, Sharmila Khan, and various others at Micron were so interesting that they kept us piqued with interest despite us hailing from the millennial generation with an attention span of hardly a few minutes. There were also interesting external sessions such as with Mr. bhaskar pramanik, the former MD of Microsoft India, and a name which needs no introduction owing to his super helpful YouTube videos especially for young minds like us, Mr. Ankur Warikoo. All these sessions rolling one after the other without any disruption were possible only due to the efforts of Anthony Marsheal Fernandes who was the curator of the Assimilation program, equally supported by Asha Menon and various others. The first week at Micron Technology, the world leader and pioneer in memory and storage solutions has shown that the oncoming journey at the company responsible for our safe and secure storage of data is going to be one full of exciting challenges and learnings constrained only by my own physical limitations. I look forward to working with my team led by Swaroop Mannepalli who will be my manager, my mentor Sashankh Ravi, my buddy Neema Davis K and various other team members with whom I look forward to interacting soon. #Micron #datascience #artificialintelligence #innovation #technology #Hyderabad #FirstJob
